# NSE API Catalog


## commodity_derivatives

| Endpoint | Params | Signal | Frequency | Priority | Collect | Used by | Bot value |
|---|---|---|---|---:|---|---|---|
| `GET /api/commodity-futures` | index=comm_der_most_act_vol | macro_commodity_context | live/intraday | 3 | no | https://www.nseindia.com/market-data/commodity-derivatives | Crude/metals/agri context for sector-sensitive equities. |
| `GET /api/commodity-futures` | type= | macro_commodity_context | live/intraday | 3 | no | https://www.nseindia.com/market-data/most-active-contracts | Crude/metals/agri context for sector-sensitive equities. |
| `GET /api/commodity-futures` | - | macro_commodity_context | live/intraday | 3 | no | https://www.nseindia.com/market-data/commodity-derivatives | Crude/metals/agri context for sector-sensitive equities. |
| `GET /api/commodity-futures` | - | macro_commodity_context | live/intraday | 3 | no | https://www.nseindia.com/market-data/most-active-contracts | Crude/metals/agri context for sector-sensitive equities. |
| `GET /api/option-chain-com` | symbol= | option_flow | live | 3 | no | https://www.nseindia.com/option-chain | Commodity derivative pressure for crude/metals-linked equity context. |
| `GET /api/quotes-commodity-derivatives-master` | - | contract_reference | static/live | 3 | no | https://www.nseindia.com/option-chain | Commodity derivative universe and contract metadata. |
